<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Marsch für des Königs Leibwache No.2
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Gerson,_Georg" title="Category:Gerson, Georg">Gerson, Georg</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>G.109
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IGG 116
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>E-flat major
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1817-06-20
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1817-10-12
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic" title="Category:Romantic">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Classical_style" title="Category:Classical style">Classical</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td><i>military band</i> <span class="expandline">
<dl><dd>2 E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span> flutes, 2 oboes, 2 E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span> clarinets, 2 clarinets (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>), 2 bassoons<br />4 horns (2 in E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>, 2 in B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>), 3 trumpets (2 in E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>, 1 in B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>),<br />bass trombone, corno basso*, serpent, bass drum, cymbals  <br />*<small>The <i>corno basso</i> was developed from the serpent around 1800. See <i>Handbuch der Musikinstrumentenkunde</i><br />by Curt Sachs (Leipzig, 1930. pp.264ff) and the German language <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/de:Basshorn" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:de:Basshorn">Wikipedia article on Basshorn</a>.</small> </span>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr></table>
